    }
  ],

      "type": "hysteria",
      "tag": "dongtaiwang.com",
      "server": "www.dtku50.xyz", 
      "server_port": 11229,
      "up_mbps": 11, 
      "down_mbps": 55,

        "enabled": true,
        "insecure": true,
